Standard GUI template for generating forms to run on a PC.
The template includes an iconic MDI toolbar, with tool tips  help, and a pre-defined set of CG$ visual attributes.

/* CGNV$CLOSE_ALL_WINDOWS */
/* Close any open windows in the form */
BEGIN
  CGNV$.nav_enter_query := FALSE;
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.MODE') = 'ENTER-QUERY') THEN
    exit_form;
  ELSE
    CGNV$.CLOSE_ALL_WINDOWS(name_in('SYSTEM.FORM_STATUS'));
  END IF;
END;

/* CGGN$KEY_CLRFRM */
/* Perform the key's standard functionality */
BEGIN
  clear_form;
  IF name_in('SYSTEM.FORM_STATUS') = 'CHANGED' THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
END;

  END IF;
END;

/* CGYR$SET_DATE_FORMAT */
/* Establish Single Standard Format Mask with 4-digit-year element */
BEGIN
  set_application_property(DATE_FORMAT_COMPATIBILITY_MODE, '5.0');
  set_application_property(PLSQL_DATE_FORMAT, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS');
  set_application_property(BUILTIN_DATE_FORMAT, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS');
  forms_ddl('ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = ''YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS''');
END;

/* CGNV$PRE_FORM_NAVCCF */
/* Set if we want to close child forms as well as child windows */
  DECLARE
  rg_id RECORDGROUP;
  gc_type GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_name GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_parent GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_tag GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_extra GROUPCOLUMN;
BEGIN
  CGNV$.nav_opening_wnd := FALSE;
  :global.CGNV_last_closed_form := '0';
  :global.CGNV_child_form := find_form(get_application_property(FORM_NAME)).id;
  rg_id := create_group('CGSH$FORM_OBJECTS');
  gc_type := add_group_column(rg_id, 'OBJECT_TYPE', CHAR_COLUMN, 2);
  gc_name := add_group_column(rg_id, 'OBJECT_NAME', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_parent := add_group_column(rg_id, 'PARENT_NAME', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_tag := add_group_column(rg_id, 'ITEM_TAG', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_extra := add_group_column(rg_id, 'EXTRA_TEXT', CHAR_COLUMN, 240);
  add_group_row(rg_id, 1);
  set_group_char_cell(gc_type, 1, 'WN');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_name, 1, 'DATE_LOV_WINDOW');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_parent, 1, '');
  add_group_row(rg_id, 2);
  set_group_char_cell(gc_type, 2, 'WN');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_name, 2, 'WINDOW');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_parent, 2, '');
END;

/* CGGN$GET_DATE_AND_USER */
/* Get the current user and date; store in items for general use */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    CURSOR C IS
      SELECT  SYSDATE, USER
      FROM    SYS.DUAL;
  BEGIN
    OPEN C;
    FETCH C
    INTO    :PARAMETER.CGU$SYSDATE, :PARAMETER.CGU$USER;
    IF C%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C;
      MESSAGE('Internal Error: No row in table SYS.DUAL');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C;
  END;
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes
   - Execution Hierarchy                             Override
   - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                      No
   - 'Keyboard Help' Text                            
   - Trigger Steps                                   
   ----------
   * Name                                            PRE-COMMIT
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   - Trigger Style                                   PL/SQL
   * Trigger Text

/*CGAP$TES_SEQUENCE_BEFORE*/
DECLARE
   v_current_block_name  pkg_mylib_form_types. subtyp_obj_name;
   c_last_block_name  CONSTANT v_current_block_name% TYPE :=
      Get_Form_Property ( :system.current_form, last_block );

   v_current_item_name  pkg_mylib_form_types. subtyp_obj_name;
   v_current_item_id  ITEM;
   v_last_item_name  v_current_item_name% TYPE;

BEGIN

   v_current_block_name :=
      Get_Form_Property ( :system.current_form, first_block );
   << Loop_All_Blocks >>
   LOOP
      IF Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, records_displayed ) > 1
      THEN

         v_last_item_name :=
            Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, last_item );

         v_current_item_name :=
            Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, first_item );
         << Loop_All_Block_Items >>
         LOOP
         	  v_current_item_id :=
         	     Find_Item
            	    ( v_current_block_name || '.' || v_current_item_name );

            IF Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id, displayed ) = 'TRUE' AND
             	 Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id, item_canvas ) IS NOT NULL AND
            	 Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id,
                    records_displayed ) > 1 -- displayed > once; this property is NEVER 0 at runtime;
            THEN
               Set_Item_Property
                  ( v_current_item_id,
                    current_record_attribute,
                    'CG$CURRENT_RECORD' ); -- "safe" to hard-code name bec this is a STD visual attr.;
            END IF;

         EXIT WHEN v_current_item_name = v_last_item_name;
            v_current_item_name :=
               Get_Item_Property ( v_current_item_id, nextitem );

         END LOOP Loop_All_Block_Items;

      END IF;

   EXIT WHEN v_current_block_name = c_last_block_name;
      v_current_block_name :=
         Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, nextblock );

   END LOOP Loop_All_Blocks;
END;

/* CGLY$COPY_USER_DATE */
/* Values from USER and DATE items on content canvas 0 in the control */
/* block will be \"fired\" to all other USER and DATE items           */
/* on other content canvas.                                           */
BEGIN
  CGBS2$.SET_COORD_STYLE( 'P' );
  CGBS2$.SET_QRY_ON_ENTRY( 'Y' );
  CGBS2$.SET_NAV_FROM_BLOCK( 'ORHD' );
  :CG$CTRL.CG$DT := :PARAMETER.CGU$SYSDATE;
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'CG$CTRL.CG$US');
END;

/* CGBS$ON_CLEAR_DETAILS */
/* clear all detail blocks for the given master block */
BEGIN
  IF (FORM_FAILURE AND name_in('SYSTEM.COORDINATION_OPERATION') IN ('MOUSE', 'DUPLICATE_RECORD')) THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.MASTER_BLOCK') = name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK')) THEN
    CGBS$.CLEAR_MASTER_DETAIL( name_in('SYSTEM.MASTER_BLOCK'), name_in('SYSTEM.COORDINATION_OPERATION') );
  END IF;
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes
   - Execution Hierarchy                             Override
   * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                      Yes
   - 'Keyboard Help' Text                            
   - Trigger Steps

   - Comments

/* CGBS$KEY_ENTQRY_FRM */
/* Check if query is allowed to avoid unnecessary coordination */
BEGIN
  IF (get_block_property( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK'), QUERY_ALLOWED) = 'FALSE') THEN
    MESSAGE('Error: Query not allowed in this block');
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  CGBS$.DO_KEYQRY( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK'), 'ENTER_QUERY', name_in('SYSTEM.MODE'));
END;

/* CGBS$KEY_CLRBLK_FRM */
/* Perform checks prior to clearing block */
BEGIN
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_RECORD_DIRTY(name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK')) ) THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.BLOCK_STATUS') = 'CHANGED' OR CGBS2$.IS_COMMIT_NEEDED( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK') ) ) THEN
    CGBS2$.DO_COMMIT_DIALOGUE;
  END IF;
  clear_block( NO_VALIDATE );
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes
   - Execution Hierarchy                             Override
   * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                      Yes
   - 'Keyboard Help' Text                            
   - Trigger Steps                                   
   ----------
   * Name                                            KEY-CLRREC
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   - Trigger Style                                   PL/SQL
   * Trigger Text                                    

/* CGBS$KEY_CLRREC */
/* Avoid clearing details if current row is new and invalid */
BEGIN
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_RECORD_DIRTY(name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK')) ) THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_COMMIT_NEEDED( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK') ) ) THEN
    CGBS2$.DO_COMMIT_DIALOGUE;
  END IF;
  clear_record;
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes

/* CGBS$TOGGLE_QUERY_MODE */
/* This changes the mode of block synchronization so that if it is */
/* currently ON, then it is changed to OFF, and vice-versa.        */
/* It also queries the dependent blocks as appropriate for the     */
/* new mode.                                                       */
BEGIN
  CGBS$TOGGLE( :GLOBAL.CG$QUERY_MODE );
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes
   - Execution Hierarchy                             Override
   * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                      Yes
   * 'Keyboard Help' Text                            Toggle Query Mode

/* CGFK$QRY_LOOKUP_DATA */
/* Query lookup data for the foreign key(s) */
BEGIN
  IF (
        (name_in('ORHD.CUST_CODE') IS NOT NULL)
     )
  THEN
    BEGIN
      CGFK$QRY_ORHD_ORHD_CUST_FK(
        :ORHD.CUST_DISCOUNT_RATE,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORHD.CUST_DISCOUNT_RATE */
        :ORHD.CUST_PAYMENT_TERM,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORHD.CUST_PAYMENT_TERM */
        :ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_TITLE,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_TITLE */
        :ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_PERSON,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_PERSON */
        :ORHD.CUST_COMPANY_NAME,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORHD.CUST_COMPANY_NAME */
        :ORHD.CUST_CODE);   /* IN : Value in item :ORHD.CUST_CODE */
    EXCEPTION
      WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: This Customer does not exist');
      WHEN OTHERS THEN
        CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
    END;
    SET_RECORD_PROPERTY(:SYSTEM.TRIGGER_RECORD, 'ORHD', STATUS , QUERY_STATUS);
  END IF;
END;
     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    Yes
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          PRE-UPDATE
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

/* CGWH$SET_AUDIT_UPD_FLDS */
/* Set the date and/or user updated items to the system date/oracle user */
BEGIN
  copy(TRUNC(SYSDATE), 'ORHD.DT_MODIFIED');
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'ORHD.MODIFIED_BY');
END;
     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    Yes
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          PRE-INSERT
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

/* CGWH$SET_AUDIT_INS_FLDS */
/* Set the date/user created/modified items to the system date/oracle user */
BEGIN
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'ORHD.CREATED_BY');
  copy(TRUNC(SYSDATE), 'ORHD.DT_CREATED');
END;
     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes

/* CGRI$CHECK_ON_DELETE */
/* This checks that the user is allowed to delete the current row, */
/* prior to removing it,  according to any referential integrity   */
/* rules held in the database design.                              */
BEGIN
  BEGIN
    CGRI$CHK_WB_OR_HDR(
      TRUE           /* IN : Check FKs validated in BOTH (client/server)? */
     ,:ORHD.OR_NO);  /* IN : Item value                                   */
  EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
      CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
  END;
END;

/* CGGN$KEY_DELREC */
/* Perform the key's standard functionality */
BEGIN
  delete_record;
  BEGIN
    CG$CHK_PACKAGE_FAILURE;
  EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
      CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
  END;
END;

     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override

     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text

    CGTE$ORHD_ERRORS;
  EXCEPTION

      CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
  END;
END;

/* CGUV$CHK_KEYS_ON_VAL_FLD */
/* Check item value against unique or primary key */
BEGIN
  IF (name_in('ORHD.OR_NO') IS NOT NULL) THEN
  CGUV$CHK_ORHD_PK(
    :ORHD.OR_NO);  /* IN : Item value */
  MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same OR No');
  RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
EXCEPTION
  WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN NULL;
  WHEN OTHERS THEN
    CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
END;

/* CGFK$QRY_LOOKUP_DATA */
/* Query lookup data for the foreign key(s) */
BEGIN
  IF (
        (name_in('ORDT.WAYBILL_NO') IS NOT NULL)
     )
  THEN
    BEGIN
      CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK(
        :ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT */
        :ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT */
        :ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT */
        :ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION */
        :ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN */
        :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE */
        :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME */
        :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME */
        :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER */
        :ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE */
        :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO);   /* IN : Value in item :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO */
    EXCEPTION
      WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: This LCL Waybill No does not exist');
      WHEN OTHERS THEN
        CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
    END;
    SET_RECORD_PROPERTY(:SYSTEM.TRIGGER_RECORD, 'ORDT', STATUS , QUERY_STATUS);
  END IF;
END;

BEGIN
  IF (
        (name_in('ORDT.HAULER_NO') IS NOT NULL)
     )
  THEN
    BEGIN
      CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_HAHD_FK(
        :ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT */
        :ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT */
        :ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT */
        :ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION */
        :ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN */
        :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE */
        :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME */
        :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME */
        :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER */
        :ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE,    /* OUT: Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE */
        :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO);   /* IN : Value in item :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO */
    EXCEPTION
      WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: This FCL Waybill No does not exist');
      WHEN OTHERS THEN
        CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
    END;
    SET_RECORD_PROPERTY(:SYSTEM.TRIGGER_RECORD, 'ORDT', STATUS , QUERY_STATUS);
  END IF;
END;

/* CGWH$SET_AUDIT_UPD_FLDS */
/* Set the date and/or user updated items to the system date/oracle user */
BEGIN
  IF :ordt.waybill_no is not null and
  	 :ordt.hauler_no is not null 
  THEN
     msg_alert('Please input on either LCL or FCL Waybill No.', 'E', TRUE);
  ELSIF :ordt.waybill_no is null and
  	 :ordt.hauler_no is null 
  THEN
     msg_alert('Please input on either LCL or FCL Waybill No.', 'E', TRUE);
  END IF;
  copy(SYSDATE, 'ORDT.DT_MODIFIED');
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'ORDT.MODIFIED_BY');
END;


     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    Yes
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          PRE-INSERT
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

/* CGWH$SET_AUDIT_INS_FLDS */
/* Set the date/user created/modified items to the system date/oracle user */
BEGIN
  IF :ordt.waybill_no is not null and
  	 :ordt.hauler_no is not null 
  THEN
     msg_alert('Please input on either LCL or FCL Waybill No.', 'E', TRUE);
  ELSIF :ordt.waybill_no is null and
  	 :ordt.hauler_no is null 
  THEN
     msg_alert('Please input on either LCL or FCL Waybill No.', 'E', TRUE);
  END IF;
  select nvl(max(item_no),0)+1 into :ordt.item_no from wb_or_dtl where or_no = :orhd.or_no;
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'ORDT.CREATED_BY');
  copy(SYSDATE, 'ORDT.DT_CREATED');
END;

     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override

/* CGTE$BLK_LEVEL_ERROR_TRAP */
/* Trap errors returning from the server and report in a user friendly manner */
BEGIN
  BEGIN
    CGTE$ORDT_ERRORS;
  EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
      CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
  END;
END;
     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    Yes
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          POST-INSERT
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

DECLARE
   nAmt Number(12,4);
BEGIN
   if :ordt.waybill_no is not null then
      select sum(amt) 
      into   nAmt
      from   wb_or_dtl
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.waybill_no;

      update wb_waybill_hdr
      set    paid_amt = nAmt,
             balance_amt  = greatest(total_amt - nAmt,0),
             payment_status = decode(greatest(total_amt - nAmt,0), 0, 'PD', decode(nAmt,0,'UN','PA'))
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.waybill_no;
   elsif :ordt.hauler_no is not null then

      select sum(amt) 
      into   nAmt
      from   wb_or_dtl
      where  hauler_no = :ordt.hauler_no;

      update wb_hauler_hdr
      set    paid_amt = nAmt,
             payment_status = decode(greatest(amt - nAmt,0), 0, 'PD', decode(nAmt,0,'UN','PA'))
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.hauler_no;
   end if;
END;

     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    No
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps

     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

DECLARE
   nAmt Number(12,4);
BEGIN
   if :ordt.waybill_no is not null then
      select sum(amt) 
      into   nAmt
      from   wb_or_dtl
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.waybill_no;

      update wb_waybill_hdr
      set    paid_amt = nAmt,
             balance_amt  = greatest(total_amt - nAmt,0),
             payment_status = decode(greatest(total_amt - nAmt,0), 0, 'PD', decode(nAmt,0,'UN','PA'))
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.waybill_no;
   elsif :ordt.hauler_no is not null then
      select sum(amt) 
      into   nAmt
      from   wb_or_dtl
      where  hauler_no = :ordt.hauler_no;

      update wb_hauler_hdr
      set    paid_amt = nAmt,
             payment_status = decode(greatest(amt - nAmt,0), 0, 'PD', decode(nAmt,0,'UN','PA'))
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.hauler_no;
   end if;

END;

DECLARE
   nAmt Number(12,4);
BEGIN
   if :ordt.waybill_no is not null then
      select sum(amt) 
      into   nAmt
      from   wb_or_dtl
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.waybill_no;

      if nAmt is null then
         nAmt := 0;
      end if;

      update wb_waybill_hdr
      set    paid_amt = nAmt,
             balance_amt  = greatest(total_amt - nAmt,0),
             payment_status = decode(greatest(total_amt - nAmt,0), 0, 'PD', decode(nAmt,0,'UN','PA'))
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.waybill_no;
   elsif :ordt.hauler_no is not null then

      select sum(amt) 
      into   nAmt
      from   wb_or_dtl
      where  hauler_no = :ordt.hauler_no;

      if nAmt is null then
         nAmt := 0;
      end if;

      update wb_hauler_hdr
      set    paid_amt = nAmt,
             payment_status = decode(greatest(amt - nAmt,0), 0, 'PD', decode(nAmt,0,'UN','PA'))
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.hauler_no;
   end if;
END;

     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    No
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          WHEN-VALIDATE-RECORD
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

begin
   if get_record_property(:system.cursor_record, 'ORDT', status) IN ('CHANGED', 'INSERT') then
      :orhd.amt := nvl(:ordt.total_amt,0);
   end if;
end;

BEGIN
  IF :ordt.waybill_no is not null and
  	 :ordt.hauler_no is not null 
  THEN
     :ordt.waybill_no := null;
     msg_alert('Clear FCL Waybill No., then enter LCL Waybill No.', 'E', TRUE);
  END IF;
END;

BEGIN
  IF (name_in('ORDT.OR_NO') IS NOT NULL OR  name_in('ORDT.WAYBILL_NO') IS NOT NULL OR name_in('ORDT.HAULER_NO') IS NOT NULL) THEN
     CGUV$CHK_ORDT_UK(
          :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO    /* IN : Item value */
         ,:ORDT.HAULER_NO     /* IN : Item value */
         ,:ORDT.OR_NO     );  /* IN : Item value */
     msg_alert('Error: Row exists already with same Or No, LCL Waybill No, FCL Waybill No', 'E', TRUE);
  ELSE
     msg_alert('Error: LCL Waybill No. or FCL Waybill No. must be entered', 'E', TRUE);
     RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;


EXCEPTION
  WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN NULL;
  WHEN OTHERS THEN
    CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
END;

BEGIN
  IF :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO IS NULL AND :ORDT.HAULER_NO IS NULL THEN
     CGSF$CLR_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK; 
     :ORDT.whdr_total_bal := 0;
  END IF;
END;


BEGIN
   :ORDT.amt := :ORDT.whdr_total_bal;
END;

       - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                    Yes
       - Execution Hierarchy                         Override
       - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                  No
       - 'Keyboard Help' Text                        
       - Trigger Steps                               
       ----------
       * Name                                        WHEN-VALIDATE-ITEM
       - Subclass Information                        
       - Comments                                    
       - Trigger Style                               PL/SQL
       * Trigger Text                                

DECLARE
   nAmt Number(12,4);
BEGIN
--   if :ordt.total_amt > :orhd.amt then
--   	  :ordt.amt := 0;
--      msg_alert('Total waybill amount exceeds OR amount.', 'E', TRUE);
--   end if;

   if :ordt.amt > nvl(:ordt.whdr_total_bal,0) then

      select nvl(sum(amt),0) 
      into   nAmt
      from   wb_or_dtl
      where  waybill_no = :ordt.waybill_no
      and    or_no <> :ordt.or_no;
      if (nAmt + :ordt.amt) > :ordt.whdr_total_amt then
         :ordt.amt := :ordt.whdr_total_amt - nAmt;
         msg_alert('Amount entered exceeds waybill remaining balance.', 'E', TRUE);
      end if;
   end if;
END;

       - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                    Yes
       - Execution Hierarchy                         Override
       - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                  No
       - 'Keyboard Help' Text                        
       - Trigger Steps

     ----------
     * Name                                          WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME
     - Item Type                                     Text Item

/*CGAP$TEMPLATE_NAMED_ROUTINE*/
PROCEDURE displayCalendar IS
BEGIN
   if Name_In ( :system.cursor_item ) is null then
      date_lov.get_date (sysdate, :system.cursor_item );
   else
      date_lov.get_date (Name_In ( :system.cursor_item ), :system.cursor_item );
   end if;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CLOSE_CURSOR_ITEM_WINDOW
   - Subclass Information                            
   * Comments                                        CG$IGNORE_ON_DESIGN_CAPTURE
   * Program Unit Text                               

PROCEDURE Close_Cursor_Item_Window
IS
BEGIN
   CGNV$. TERMINATE_WINDOW
      ( Get_View_Property
           ( Get_Item_Property
                ( :system.cursor_item, item_canvas ),
             window_name ),
        Name_In('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_ITEM'),
        Name_In('SYSTEM.FORM_STATUS'),
        FALSE );
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            MSG_ALERT
   - Subclass Information                            
   * Comments                                        CG$IGNORE_ON_DESIGN_CAPTURE
   * Program Unit Text                               

procedure msg_alert(
errm in VARCHAR2,           /* message */
errt in VARCHAR2,           /* message type */
rftf in boolean         /* raise form_trigger_failure ? */
) is      /* message parameters */
/*
* ----------------------------------------------------------------
* CHANGE HISTORY:
* DATE   PERSON      CHANGE
* ------ ----------- ---------------------------------------------
*
*/

alert_is alert;
alert_button number;

BEGIN

     IF (errt = 'F')
     THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_SYSTEM_ERROR');
     ELSIF (errt = 'E')
        THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_ERROR');
        ELSIF (errt = 'W')
           THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_WARNING_A');
              ELSIF (errt = 'I')
                 THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_INFORMATION');
                    ELSIF (errt = '2')
	                	THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_2BUTTON');
				               ELSIF (errt = '3')
        			         THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_3BUTTON');
					                 ELSE MESSAGE(errm);
     end if;

     IF (errt IN ('F','E','W','I'))
     THEN SET_ALERT_PROPERTY(alert_is,ALERT_MESSAGE_TEXT,errm);
          alert_button := SHOW_ALERT(alert_is);
     END IF;

     IF (rftf)
     THEN
       RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
     END IF;


END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGSF$CLR_ORHD_ORHD_CUST_FK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGSF$CLR_ORHD_ORHD_CUST_FK */
/* This clears all items associated with the given foreign key. */
PROCEDURE CGSF$CLR_ORHD_ORHD_CUST_FK IS
BEGIN
  IF (NAME_IN('ORHD.CUST_DISCOUNT_RATE') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORHD.CUST_DISCOUNT_RATE');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORHD.CUST_PAYMENT_TERM') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORHD.CUST_PAYMENT_TERM');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_TITLE') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_TITLE');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_PERSON') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_PERSON');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORHD.CUST_COMPANY_NAME') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORHD.CUST_COMPANY_NAME');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORHD.CUST_CODE') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORHD.CUST_CODE');
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGFK$QRY_ORHD_ORHD_CUST_FK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGFK$QRY_ORHD_ORHD_CUST_FK */
/* Query foreign key value/query lookup data. */
PROCEDURE CGFK$QRY_ORHD_ORHD_CUST_FK(
   P_CUST_DISCOUNT_RATE   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORHD.CUST_DISCOUNT_RATE */
   P_CUST_PAYMENT_TERM   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORHD.CUST_PAYMENT_TERM */
   P_CUST_CONTACT_TITLE   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_TITLE */
   P_CUST_CONTACT_PERSON   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORHD.CUST_CONTACT_PERSON */
   P_CUST_COMPANY_NAME   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORHD.CUST_COMPANY_NAME */
   P_CUST_CODE   IN VARCHAR2   /* Value in item :ORHD.CUST_CODE */
)
IS
  CURSOR C1 IS
    SELECT CUST.DISCOUNT_RATE
          ,CUST.PAYMENT_TERM
          ,CUST.CONTACT_TITLE
          ,CUST.CONTACT_PERSON
          ,CUST.COMPANY_NAME
    FROM   WB_CUSTOMER CUST
    WHERE  P_CUST_CODE = CUST.CODE
    ;

BEGIN

    OPEN C1;
    FETCH C1
    INTO
         P_CUST_DISCOUNT_RATE,
         P_CUST_PAYMENT_TERM,
         P_CUST_CONTACT_TITLE,
         P_CUST_CONTACT_PERSON,
         P_CUST_COMPANY_NAME;
    IF C1%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C1;
      RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C1;

END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGUV$CHK_ORHD_PK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGUV$CHK_ORHD_PK */
PROCEDURE CGUV$CHK_ORHD_PK(
   P_OR_NO IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Item value */
/* Check uniqueness against primary/unique constraint        */
/* Note : NO_DATA_FOUND exception handled by calling trigger */
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);
BEGIN
    DECLARE
      CURSOR C IS
        SELECT  '1'
        FROM    WB_OR_HDR
        WHERE   OR_NO = P_OR_NO;
    BEGIN
      OPEN C;
      FETCH C
      INTO    CG$DUMMY;
      IF C%NOTFOUND THEN
        CLOSE C;
        RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
      END IF;
      CLOSE C;
    END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK */
/* Query foreign key value/query lookup data. */
PROCEDURE CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK(
   P_WHDR_BALANCE_AMT   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT */
   P_WHDR_PAID_AMT   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT */
   P_WHDR_TOTAL_AMT   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT */
   P_WHDR_DESTINATION   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION */
   P_WHDR_ORIGIN   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN */
   P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE */
   P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME */
   P_WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME */
   P_WHDR_SHIPPER   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER */
   P_WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE   OUT DATE, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE */
   P_WAYBILL_NO   IN VARCHAR2   /* Value in item :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO */
)
IS
  CURSOR C1 IS
    SELECT greatest(nvl(WHDR.TOTAL_AMT,0)-nvl(WHDR.PAID_AMT,0),0) BALANCE_AMT
          ,WHDR.PAID_AMT
          ,WHDR.TOTAL_AMT
          ,WHDR.DESTINATION
          ,WHDR.ORIGIN
          ,WHDR.CONSIGNEE
          ,WHDR.CONSIGNEE_NAME
          ,WHDR.SHIPPER_NAME
          ,WHDR.SHIPPER
          ,WHDR.WAYBILL_DATE
    FROM   WB_WAYBILL_HDR WHDR
    WHERE  P_WAYBILL_NO = WHDR.WAYBILL_NO
    ;

BEGIN

    OPEN C1;
    FETCH C1
    INTO
         P_WHDR_BALANCE_AMT,
         P_WHDR_PAID_AMT,
         P_WHDR_TOTAL_AMT,
         P_WHDR_DESTINATION,
         P_WHDR_ORIGIN,
         P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE,
         P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME,
         P_WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME,
         P_WHDR_SHIPPER,
         P_WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE;
    IF C1%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C1;
      RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C1;

END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGRI$CHK_WB_OR_HDR
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGRI$CHK_WB_OR_HDR */
PROCEDURE CGRI$CHK_WB_OR_HDR(
   P_CHECK_BOTH IN BOOLEAN       /* Check FKs validated in BOTH (client/server)? */
  ,P_OR_NO      IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Item value                                   */
/* Validate that the deletion of the record is permitted    */
/* by checking for the existence of rows in related tables. */
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);  /* Dummy variable */
BEGIN
  /* Deletion of WB_OR_HDR prevented if WB_OR_DTL records exist */
  /* Foreign key(s): ORDT_ORHD_FK                               */
  DECLARE
    CURSOR C IS
      SELECT  '1'
      FROM    WB_OR_DTL ORDT
      WHERE   ORDT.OR_NO = P_OR_NO;
  BEGIN
    OPEN C;
    FETCH C
    INTO    CG$DUMMY;
    IF C%FOUND THEN
      CLOSE C;
      MESSAGE('Error: Cannot delete ORs while dependent ORs exists');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C;
  END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO */
FUNCTION CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(
   P_SERVER_ERR IN NUMBER        /* Server error message */
  ,P_SERVER_MSG IN VARCHAR2)     /* Server error number  */
RETURN BOOLEAN IS
/* Check and report Primary/Unique Key, Check Constraint and User */
/* Defined Constraint violations                                  */
  constraint_name VARCHAR2(61);  /* Violated constraint */
BEGIN
  /* Check if the error code is one we are interested in */
  IF ( NOT (P_SERVER_ERR IN  (1, 2290) OR
           (P_SERVER_ERR >= 20000 AND P_SERVER_ERR <= 20999) ) )
  THEN
    RETURN( FALSE );
  END IF;

  /* Deal with user defined errors */
  IF (P_SERVER_ERR >= 20000 AND P_SERVER_ERR <= 20999) THEN
    MESSAGE('Error: '||CGTE$STRIP_FIRST_ERROR(P_SERVER_MSG));
    RETURN( TRUE );
  END IF;

  /* Deal with Primary/Unique Key and Check Constraint violations */
  constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(P_SERVER_MSG);
  IF (P_SERVER_ERR = 1) THEN
    IF (constraint_name = 'ORHD_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same OR No');
    ELSIF (constraint_name = 'CUST_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same ');
    ELSIF (constraint_name = 'ORDT_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same Or No,Waybill No');
    ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same Waybill No');
    ELSE
      MESSAGE(P_SERVER_MSG);
    END IF;
  ELSIF (P_SERVER_ERR = 2290) THEN
    MESSAGE(P_SERVER_MSG);
  END IF;
  RETURN( TRUE );
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Function
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$ORHD_ERRORS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$ORHD_ERRORS */
PROCEDURE CGTE$ORHD_ERRORS IS
/* Trap errors returning from the server and report in a user friendly manner */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    err_code        CONSTANT NUMBER         := ERROR_CODE;
    err_type        CONSTANT VARCHAR2(3)    := ERROR_TYPE;
    server_err               NUMBER         := abs(DBMS_ERROR_CODE);
    server_msg               VARCHAR2(2000) := DBMS_ERROR_TEXT;
    constraint_name          VARCHAR2(61);
  BEGIN
    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code IN (40506, 40508, 40509, 40510) ) THEN

      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* Check and report the generic constraint violations */
      IF ( CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(server_err, server_msg) ) THEN
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* Check and report the constraint violations specific to this block */
      constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(server_msg);

      /* FK - Parent key not found */
      IF (server_err = 2291) THEN
        IF (constraint_name = 'ORHD_CUST_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Customer does not exist');
        ELSE
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* FK - Child record found */
      IF (server_err = 2292) THEN
        IF (err_code = 40510) THEN
          IF (constraint_name = 'ORDT_ORHD_FK') THEN
            MESSAGE('Error: Cannot delete ORs while dependent ORs exists');
          ELSE
            MESSAGE(server_msg);
          END IF;
        ELSIF (err_code = 40509) THEN
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;
    END IF;

    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code = 40735  AND
        server_err != 0 ) THEN


      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* If error not found, issue default message */
      MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(server_err)||': '||server_msg);
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;

    /* If error not found, issue default message */
    MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(err_code)||': '||ERROR_TEXT);
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;

  END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$ORDT_ERRORS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$ORDT_ERRORS */
PROCEDURE CGTE$ORDT_ERRORS IS
/* Trap errors returning from the server and report in a user friendly manner */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    err_code        CONSTANT NUMBER         := ERROR_CODE;
    err_type        CONSTANT VARCHAR2(3)    := ERROR_TYPE;
    server_err               NUMBER         := abs(DBMS_ERROR_CODE);
    server_msg               VARCHAR2(2000) := DBMS_ERROR_TEXT;
    constraint_name          VARCHAR2(61);
  BEGIN
    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code IN (40506, 40508, 40509, 40510) ) THEN

      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* Check and report the generic constraint violations */
      IF ( CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(server_err, server_msg) ) THEN
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* Check and report the constraint violations specific to this block */
      constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(server_msg);

      /* FK - Parent key not found */
      IF (server_err = 2291) THEN
        IF (constraint_name = 'ORDT_WHDR_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Waybill No does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'ORDT_ORHD_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Or No does not exist');
        ELSE
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* FK - Child record found */
      IF (server_err = 2292) THEN
        IF (err_code = 40510) THEN
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        ELSIF (err_code = 40509) THEN
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;
    END IF;

    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code IN (41105, 41106) ) THEN
      IF (err_code = 41105) THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Query of ORs must be in context of ORs');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    ELSIF (err_code = 41106) THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Insert of ORs must be in context of ORs');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;
    END IF;

    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code = 40735  AND
        server_err != 0 ) THEN


      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* If error not found, issue default message */
      MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(server_err)||': '||server_msg);
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;

    /* If error not found, issue default message */
    MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(err_code)||': '||ERROR_TEXT);
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;

  END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES */
PROCEDURE CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES(
   P_CANVAS_LIST    IN OUT VARCHAR2      /* List of displayed canvases */
  ,P_CURRENT_CANVAS IN     VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas             */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS    IN     VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas                */
/* Display the current canvas plus any others in the canvas list */
  canvas_list VARCHAR2(255);  /* List of displayed canvases */
  canvas_to_raise VARCHAR2(255);  /* Canvas to raise to the top */
BEGIN
  IF ( P_CURRENT_CANVAS = P_BASE_CANVAS) THEN
    P_CANVAS_LIST := P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',';
  ELSE
    P_CANVAS_LIST := replace(P_CANVAS_LIST, P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',');
    IF ( get_view_property(P_BASE_CANVAS, VISIBLE) = 'FALSE') THEN
      canvas_list := P_CANVAS_LIST;
      WHILE (canvas_list IS NOT NULL) LOOP
        canvas_to_raise := substr(canvas_list, 1, instr(canvas_list, ','));
        canvas_list := replace(canvas_list, canvas_to_raise);
        CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(rtrim(canvas_to_raise, ','), P_BASE_CANVAS);
      END LOOP;
    END IF;
    P_CANVAS_LIST := P_CANVAS_LIST || P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',';
  END IF;
  CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, P_BASE_CANVAS);
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES */
PROCEDURE CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES(
   P_CURRENT_CANVAS IN OUT VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS    IN OUT VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas    */
/* Find the canvases associated with the current canvas and record which */
/* base canvas is displayed in each window                               */
BEGIN
  IF ( P_CURRENT_CANVAS = 'CG$SPREAD_TABLE_1') THEN
    P_CURRENT_CANVAS := 'CG$PAGE_1';
  END IF;
  /* CFLT */
  P_BASE_CANVAS := P_CURRENT_CANVAS;
  IF (get_view_property(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, WINDOW_NAME) = 'DATE_LOV_WINDOW') THEN
    copy(P_BASE_CANVAS, 'CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWDATE_LOV_WINDOW_PAGE');
  ELSIF (get_view_property(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, WINDOW_NAME) = 'WINDOW') THEN
    IF (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWWINDOW_PAGE') IS NULL OR name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWWINDOW_PAGE') != P_BASE_CANVAS) THEN
      set_view_property('CG$SPREAD_TABLE_1', VISIBLE, PROPERTY_OFF);
    END IF;
    copy(P_BASE_CANVAS, 'CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWWINDOW_PAGE');
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS */
PROCEDURE CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(
   P_CANVAS      IN VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas    */
/* Raise the current canvas, plus any dependant canvases to the top */
BEGIN
  set_view_property(P_CANVAS, VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
  IF ( P_BASE_CANVAS = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
    set_view_property('CG$SPREAD_TABLE_1', VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
    set_view_property('CG$STACKED_HEADER_1', VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT */
PROCEDURE CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT IS
/* Top level canvas management procedure */
  current_canvas VARCHAR2(61) := get_item_property(name_in('SYSTEM.CURSOR_ITEM'), ITEM_CANVAS);
  base_canvas VARCHAR2(61);
  canvas_list VARCHAR2(255);
BEGIN
  IF ( (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS') IS NULL) OR (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS') != current_canvas) ) THEN
    copy(current_canvas, 'CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS');
    set_window_property( get_view_property( current_canvas, WINDOW_NAME ), VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
    CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES(current_canvas, base_canvas);
    IF ( base_canvas = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
      canvas_list := name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$PAGE_1_LIST');
    END IF;
    CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES(canvas_list, current_canvas, base_canvas);
    IF ( base_canvas = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
      copy(canvas_list, 'CG$CTRL.CG$PAGE_1_LIST');
    END IF;
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$TOGGLE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$TOGGLE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$TOGGLE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN OUT VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Toggle query mode between BSMON and BSMOFF, set all query mode items, */
/* display query mode message, set the relations and ensure that the     */
/* canvas is coordinated.                                                */
BEGIN
  /* Toggle the mode */
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE != 'A') THEN
    P_QUERY_MODE := 'A';
  ELSE
    P_QUERY_MODE := 'N';
  END IF;
  /* Set all the items */
  CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* Display query mode messages */
  CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* Set the relations */
  CGBS$.SET_RELATIONS( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* If the query mode is AutoQuery, coordinate outstanding blocks */
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE = 'A') THEN
    CGBS$.COORD_VISIBLE_BLKS( name_in('SYSTEM.CURSOR_BLOCK') );
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Set all query items to the current query mode */
BEGIN
  NULL;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Send a message to the status line indicating the current query mode */
BEGIN
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE = 'A') THEN
    NULL;
  ELSE
    MESSAGE('Auto-query mode off');
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGUV$CHK_ORDT_UK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGUV$CHK_ORDT_UK */
PROCEDURE CGUV$CHK_ORDT_UK(
   P_WAYBILL_NO IN VARCHAR2      /* Item value */
  ,P_HAULER_NO  IN VARCHAR2      /* Item value */
  ,P_OR_NO      IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Item value */
/* Check uniqueness against primary/unique constraint        */
/* Note : NO_DATA_FOUND exception handled by calling trigger */
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);
BEGIN
    DECLARE
      CURSOR C IS
        SELECT  '1'
        FROM    WB_OR_DTL
        WHERE   OR_NO = P_OR_NO
        AND     HAULER_NO = P_HAULER_NO
        AND     WAYBILL_NO = P_WAYBILL_NO;
    BEGIN
      OPEN C;
      FETCH C
      INTO    CG$DUMMY;
      IF C%NOTFOUND THEN
        CLOSE C;
        RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
      END IF;
      CLOSE C;
    END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_HAHD_FK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_HAHD_FK */
/* Query foreign key value/query lookup data. */
PROCEDURE CGFK$QRY_ORDT_ORDT_HAHD_FK(
   P_WHDR_BALANCE_AMT   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT */
   P_WHDR_PAID_AMT   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT */
   P_WHDR_TOTAL_AMT   OUT NUMBER, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT */
   P_WHDR_DESTINATION   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION */
   P_WHDR_ORIGIN   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN */
   P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE */
   P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME */
   P_WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME */
   P_WHDR_SHIPPER   OUT VARCHAR2, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER */
   P_WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE   OUT DATE, /* Value in item :ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE */
   P_WAYBILL_NO   IN VARCHAR2   /* Value in item :ORDT.WAYBILL_NO */
)
IS
  CURSOR C1 IS
    SELECT WHDR.AMT-WHDR.PAID_AMT
          ,WHDR.PAID_AMT
          ,WHDR.AMT
          ,WHDR.DESTINATION
          ,WHDR.ORIGIN
          ,WHDR.CONSIGNEE
          ,WHDR.CONSIGNEE_NAME
          ,WHDR.SHIPPER_NAME
          ,WHDR.SHIPPER
          ,WHDR.WAYBILL_DATE
    FROM   WB_HAULER_HDR WHDR
    WHERE  P_WAYBILL_NO = WHDR.WAYBILL_NO
    ;

BEGIN

    OPEN C1;
    FETCH C1
    INTO
         P_WHDR_BALANCE_AMT,
         P_WHDR_PAID_AMT,
         P_WHDR_TOTAL_AMT,
         P_WHDR_DESTINATION,
         P_WHDR_ORIGIN,
         P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE,
         P_WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME,
         P_WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME,
         P_WHDR_SHIPPER,
         P_WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE;
    IF C1%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C1;
      RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C1;

END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGSF$CLR_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGSF$CLR_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK */
/* This clears all items associated with the given foreign key. */
PROCEDURE CGSF$CLR_ORDT_ORDT_WHDR_FK IS
BEGIN
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_BALANCE_AMT');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_PAID_AMT');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_TOTAL_AMT');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_DESTINATION');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_ORIGIN');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_CONSIGNEE_NAME');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER_NAME');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_SHIPPER');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WHDR_WAYBILL_DATE');
  END IF;
  IF (NAME_IN('ORDT.WAYBILL_NO') IS NOT NULL) THEN
    COPY(NULL, 'ORDT.WAYBILL_NO');
  END IF;
END;

   * Record Group Type                               Query
   o Record Group Query                              SELECT WHDR.WAYBILL_NO WAYBILL_NO,
       WHDR.WAYBILL_DATE WAYBILL_DATE,
       WHDR.SHIPPER SHIPPER,
       WHDR.SHIPPER_NAME SHIPPER_NAME,
       WHDR.CONSIGNEE CONSIGNEE,
       WHDR.CONSIGNEE_NAME CONSIGNEE_NAME,
       WHDR.ORIGIN ORIGIN,
       WHDR.DESTINATION DESTINATION,
       SUM(WHDT.TOTAL_AMT) - WHDR.PAID_AMT TOTAL_BAL,
       SUM(WHDT.TOTAL_AMT) TOTAL_AMT,
       SUM(WHDT.QTY) TOTAL_QTY,
       SUM(WHDT.WGT) TOTAL_WGT,
       SUM(WHDT.CBM) TOTAL_CBM
FROM WB_WAYBILL_HDR WHDR, WB_WAYBILL_DTL WHDT
WHERE WHDR.WAYBILL_NO = WHDT.WAYBILL_NO
AND WHDR.STATUS <> 'CN'
AND WHDR.SHIPPER = :ORHD.CUST_CODE
AND WHDR.PAYMENT_STATUS <> 'PD'
AND WHDR.PAYMENT_MODE in ('AO', 'PO')
GROUP BY WHDR.WAYBILL_NO ,
       WHDR.WAYBILL_DATE ,
       WHDR.SHIPPER,
       WHDR.SHIPPER_NAME,
       WHDR.CONSIGNEE,
       WHDR.CONSIGNEE_NAME ,
       WHDR.ORIGIN ,
       WHDR.DESTINATION,
       WHDR.PAID_AMT 
UNION
SELECT WHDR.WAYBILL_NO WAYBILL_NO,
       WHDR.WAYBILL_DATE WAYBILL_DATE,
       WHDR.SHIPPER SHIPPER,
       WHDR.SHIPPER_NAME SHIPPER_NAME,
       WHDR.CONSIGNEE CONSIGNEE,
       WHDR.CONSIGNEE_NAME CONSIGNEE_NAME,
       WHDR.ORIGIN ORIGIN,
       WHDR.DESTINATION DESTINATION,
       SUM(WHDT.TOTAL_AMT) - WHDR.PAID_AMT  TOTAL_BAL,
       SUM(WHDT.TOTAL_AMT) TOTAL_AMT,
       SUM(WHDT.QTY) TOTAL_QTY,
       SUM(WHDT.WGT) TOTAL_WGT,
       SUM(WHDT.CBM) TOTAL_CBM
FROM WB_WAYBILL_HDR WHDR, WB_WAYBILL_DTL WHDT
WHERE WHDR.WAYBILL_NO = WHDT.WAYBILL_NO
AND WHDR.STATUS <> 'CN'
AND WHDR.CONSIGNEE = :ORHD.CUST_CODE
AND WHDR.PAYMENT_STATUS <> 'PD'
AND WHDR.PAYMENT_MODE IN ('AD', 'PD')
GROUP BY WHDR.WAYBILL_NO ,
       WHDR.WAYBILL_DATE ,

       WHDR.CONSIGNEE,
